I had to ask him what my prescription was because all he was talking about was buying contacts from him during the entire exam. He mentioned that my current lenses, Aquacomfort Dailies, were subpar to the specialty lenses which are $100 a box as opposed to my usual $60. I kept feeling like he was trying to sell me. When I asked how much it would be to order them through him, I was first upfront by saying "I normally order online and use the prescription you give me because I've gotten a better price." And he continues to scoff, "Well we'll definitely beat their prices because we have rebates." Peggy, his other associate, was trying to say it would cost $490 out of pocket and I could hear him in the back asking her, "Are you sure about this price?" < review>
Half-way decent pizza hole with some other stuff and limited beer selection.  Prices are good.  $18 for an 18" pie with 1 topping.  We got the inflation beater which included 1-18" large pizza with one topping, 6 garlic breads, 1-family style spaghetti, and 1-family size salad all for $32.  This was enough food for the whole family and we had a little extra to take home.  As far as quality of food goes... Well, it wasn't amazing by any means.  The sauce was bland but not bad.  The pizza was good.  Salty, greasy and authentic house made pizza with real cheese (although light).  The salad was fresh, although the tomatoes were not ripe.  The short of it, I would go again.  Not great, but good.<//review>

Excellent food w/great pricing & service. Has a very nice down home country atmosphere. Very quaint & the help makes 1 feel as if your visiting family being & served by your Aunt Millie !! The place doesn't seem to be very big from the exterior, but, once inside you'll find, to your surprise enough room for about 10-11 tables in the front w/an additional area in the rear w/approximately 8-10 tables moderately sized. 2, or 3 tables for 2 & the rest tables for 4 w/an option & room for tables to be put together seating 8 very comfortably. My 1st time visit & won't be my last.< /Review>
